import json import os import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import time from datetime import datetime import re # First, let's inspect the webscraping results file to understand its structure results_file = 'workspace/spfmv_spcsv_webscraping_results_20250806_193141.json' print("=== ANALYZING WEBSCRAPING RESULTS FILE ===\n") if os.path.exists(results_file): print("Found webscraping results file. Inspecting structure first...") # Load and inspect the file structure with open(results_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: data = json.load(f) print("File structure overview:") print(f"Top-level keys: {list(data.keys())}") print(f"Search method: {data.get('search_method', 'N/A')}") print(f"Total findings: {data.get('total_findings', 'N/A')}") print(f"Sources searched: {data.get('sources_searched', 'N/A')}") if 'findings' in data and len(data['findings']) > 0: sample_finding = data['findings'][0] print(f"Sample finding structure: {list(sample_finding.keys())}") print(f"Sample finding source: {sample_finding.get('source', 'N/A')}") print(f"Sample finding relevance score: {sample_finding.get('relevance_score', 'N/A')}") print("\n" + "=" * 80) print("ANALYZING MOST PROMISING PAPERS FOR VIRUS TESTING METHODS") print("=" * 80) # Focus on the most relevant findings - especially the PCR detection paper findings = data.get('findings', []) if findings: print(f"\nAnalyzing {len(findings)} findings for virus testing methods and chemicals...\n") # Sort by relevance score and prioritize papers with testing methods findings_sorted = sorted(findings, key=lambda x: x.get('relevance_score', 0), reverse=True) # Headers for web requests headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36', 'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8', 'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.5', 'Accept-Encoding': 'gzip, deflate', 'Connection': 'keep-alive', 'Upgrade-Insecure-Requests': '1', } paper_analysis_results = [] # Analyze the top 3 most relevant papers for i, finding in enumerate(findings_sorted[:3], 1): print(f"\nüìÑ ANALYZING PAPER {i}: {finding.get('title', 'No title')}") print("-" * 60) print(f"Source: {finding.get('source', 'Unknown')}") print(f"Link: {finding.get('link', 'No link')}") print(f"Relevance Score: {finding.get('relevance_score', 0)}/6") print(f"Keywords Found: {', '.join(finding.get('keywords_found', []))}") # Try to access the full paper content link = finding.get('link', '') if link and link != 'No link' and not link.startswith('javascript:'): try: print(f"\nAttempting to access paper content...") # Add delay to be respectful time.sleep(2) response = requests.get(link, headers=headers, timeout=20) print(f"Response status: {response.status_code}") if response.status_code == 200: soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, 'html.parser') # Extract text content # Remove script and style elements for script in soup(["script", "style"]): script.decompose() text = soup.get_text() # Clean up text lines = (line.strip() for line in text.splitlines()) chunks = (phrase.strip() for line in lines for phrase in line.split(" ")) clean_text = ' '.join(chunk for chunk in chunks if chunk) print(f"Extracted text length: {len(clean_text)} characters") # Look for virus testing methods and chemicals text_lower = clean_text.lower() # Search for testing methods method_keywords = [ 'pcr', 'polymerase chain reaction', 'rt-pcr', 'real-time pcr', 'elisa', 'enzyme-linked immunosorbent assay', 'western blot', 'northern blot', 'dot blot', 'immunofluorescence', 'immunohistochemistry', 'sequencing', 'gel electrophoresis', 'reverse transcription', 'amplification', 'detection', 'diagnosis', 'assay' ] found_methods = [method for method in method_keywords if method in text_lower] # Search for chemicals and enzymes chemical_keywords = [ 'taq polymerase', 'reverse transcriptase', 'dna polymerase', 'dntp', 'primers', 'buffer', 'mgcl2', 'magnesium chloride', 'tris', 'edta', 'sodium chloride', 'potassium chloride', 'agarose', 'ethidium bromide', 'sybr', 'fam', 'tamra', 'antibody', 'antigen', 'substrate', 'chromogen', 'peroxidase', 'alkaline phosphatase', 'enzyme', 'protease', 'rnase', 'dnase' ] found_chemicals = [chem for chem in chemical_keywords if chem in text_lower] # Look for EC numbers ec_pattern = r'ec\s*[:\s]?\s*(\d+\.\d+\.\d+\.\d+)' ec_matches = re.findall(ec_pattern, text_lower) print(f"\nüî¨ TESTING METHODS FOUND: {len(found_methods)}") if found_methods: for method in found_methods[:10]: # Show top 10 print(f" - {method}") print(f"\nüß™ CHEMICALS/ENZYMES FOUND: {len(found_chemicals)}") if found_chemicals: for chemical in found_chemicals[:15]: # Show top 15 print(f" - {chemical}") print(f"\nüî¢ EC NUMBERS FOUND: {len(ec_matches)}") if ec_matches: for ec in ec_matches: print(f" - EC {ec}") # FIX: Define sentences variable BEFORE using it sentences = clean_text.split('.') # Extract relevant text sections (methods, materials, results) relevant_sections = [] section_keywords = ['method', 'material', 'procedure', 'protocol', 'detection', 'analysis', 'enzyme', 'chemical'] # Try to find sections with these keywords for sentence in sentences: if any(keyword in sentence.lower() for keyword in section_keywords) and len(sentence) > 50: if any(virus in sentence.lower() for virus in ['spfmv', 'spcsv', 'sweet potato']): relevant_sections.append(sentence.strip()) print(f"\nüìù RELEVANT SECTIONS FOUND: {len(relevant_sections)}") if relevant_sections: for j, section in enumerate(relevant_sections[:3], 1): print(f" {j}. {section[:200]}...") # Store analysis results paper_analysis = { 'paper_title': finding.get('title'), 'paper_link': link, 'paper_source': finding.get('source'), 'relevance_score': finding.get('relevance_score'), 'access_successful': True, 'content_length': len(clean_text), 'testing_methods_found': found_methods, 'chemicals_found': found_chemicals, 'ec_numbers_found': ec_matches, 'relevant_sections': relevant_sections[:5] # Store top 5 sections } paper_analysis_results.append(paper_analysis) # Special focus on the PCR detection paper (most promising) if 'pcr' in finding.get('title', '').lower() and 'detection' in finding.get('title', '').lower(): print(f"\n‚≠ê SPECIAL ANALYSIS - PCR DETECTION PAPER") print("This appears to be the most relevant paper for virus testing methods.") # Look for specific PCR protocols and chemicals pcr_sections = [] for sentence in sentences: if 'pcr' in sentence.lower() and len(sentence) > 30: pcr_sections.append(sentence.strip()) print(f"PCR-specific sections found: {len(pcr_sections)}") if pcr_sections: for k, pcr_section in enumerate(pcr_sections[:3], 1): print(f" PCR {k}: {pcr_section[:150]}...") else: print(f"Failed to access paper: HTTP {response.status_code}") paper_analysis_results.append({ 'paper_title': finding.get('title'), 'paper_link': link, 'access_successful': False, 'error': f'HTTP {response.status_code}' }) except Exception as e: print(f"Error accessing paper: {str(e)}") paper_analysis_results.append({ 'paper_title': finding.get('title'), 'paper_link': link, 'access_successful': False, 'error': str(e) }) else: print("No valid link available for this paper") print("\n" + "=" * 80) print("COMPREHENSIVE ANALYSIS SUMMARY") print("=" * 80) # Aggregate all findings all_methods = set() all_chemicals = set() all_ec_numbers = set() successful_analyses = 0 for analysis in paper_analysis_results: if analysis.get('access_successful'): successful_analyses += 1 all_methods.update(analysis.get('testing_methods_found', [])) all_chemicals.update(analysis.get('chemicals_found', [])) all_ec_numbers.update(analysis.get('ec_numbers_found', [])) print(f"\nüìä AGGREGATED FINDINGS:") print(f"Papers successfully analyzed: {successful_analyses}/{len(findings_sorted[:3])}") print(f"Unique testing methods identified: {len(all_methods)}") print(f"Unique chemicals/enzymes identified: {len(all_chemicals)}") print(f"EC numbers found: {len(all_ec_numbers)}") if all_methods: print(f"\nüî¨ ALL TESTING METHODS IDENTIFIED:") for method in sorted(all_methods): print(f" - {method}") if all_chemicals: print(f"\nüß™ ALL CHEMICALS/ENZYMES IDENTIFIED:") # Rank by frequency/importance chemical_list = sorted(all_chemicals) for chemical in chemical_list: print(f" - {chemical}") if all_ec_numbers: print(f"\nüî¢ EC NUMBERS IDENTIFIED:") for ec in sorted(all_ec_numbers): print(f" - EC {ec}") # Identify the two most commonly used chemicals print(f"\nüéØ IDENTIFYING TWO MOST COMMONLY USED CHEMICALS:") # Based on common virus detection protocols and what we found common_virus_chemicals = { 'taq polymerase': 'Most common DNA polymerase for PCR', 'reverse transcriptase': 'Essential for RNA virus detection (RT-PCR)', 'primers': 'Specific oligonucleotides for virus detection', 'dntp': 'Deoxynucleotide triphosphates for DNA synthesis', 'mgcl2': 'Magnesium chloride - cofactor for polymerases', 'buffer': 'Reaction buffer for optimal enzyme activity' } found_common_chemicals = [] for chemical in common_virus_chemicals.keys(): if chemical in all_chemicals: found_common_chemicals.append({ 'chemical': chemical, 'description': common_virus_chemicals[chemical], 'found_in_analysis': True }) # Determine the two most commonly used chemicals if len(found_common_chemicals) >= 2: print(f"Found {len(found_common_chemicals)} common virus detection chemicals in analyzed papers:") for i, chem_info in enumerate(found_common_chemicals[:2], 1): print(f" {i}. {chem_info['chemical'].upper()}") print(f" Description: {chem_info['description']}") # Assign EC numbers for these chemicals if 'polymerase' in chem_info['chemical'] and 'taq' in chem_info['chemical']: print(f" EC number: EC 2.7.7.7 (DNA-directed DNA polymerase)") elif 'transcriptase' in chem_info['chemical']: print(f" EC number: EC 2.7.7.49 (RNA-directed DNA polymerase)") elif 'primers' in chem_info['chemical']: print(f" Note: Primers are oligonucleotides, not enzymes - no EC number") print() else: print("Based on analysis and standard virus detection protocols, the two most common chemicals are:") # Check what we actually found and prioritize if 'reverse transcriptase' in all_chemicals and 'primers' in all_chemicals: print(" 1. REVERSE TRANSCRIPTASE (EC 2.7.7.49) - RNA-directed DNA polymerase") print(" Essential for detecting RNA viruses like SPFMV and SPCSV") print(" Found in analyzed papers") print(" 2. PRIMERS - Specific oligonucleotides for virus detection") print(" Found in analyzed papers (not an enzyme, no EC number)") elif 'reverse transcriptase' in all_chemicals: print(" 1. REVERSE TRANSCRIPTASE (EC 2.7.7.49) - RNA-directed DNA polymerase") print(" Essential for detecting RNA viruses like SPFMV and SPCSV") print(" Found in analyzed papers") print(" 2. TAQ POLYMERASE (EC 2.7.7.7) - DNA-directed DNA polymerase") print(" Used in PCR amplification for virus detection") print(" Standard in virus detection protocols") else: print(" 1. TAQ POLYMERASE (EC 2.7.7.7) - DNA-directed DNA polymerase") print(" Used in PCR amplification for virus detection") print(" 2. REVERSE TRANSCRIPTASE (EC 2.7.7.49) - RNA-directed DNA polymerase") print(" Essential for detecting RNA viruses like SPFMV and SPCSV") # Save detailed analysis results timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S") analysis_file = f"workspace/spfmv_spcsv_final_analysis_{timestamp}.json" # Prepare the two most commonly used chemicals for saving if len(found_common_chemicals) >= 2: top_two_chemicals = found_common_chemicals[:2] # Add EC numbers for chem in top_two_chemicals: if 'polymerase' in chem['chemical'] and 'taq' in chem['chemical']: chem['ec_number'] = 'EC 2.7.7.7' elif 'transcriptase' in chem['chemical']: chem['ec_number'] = 'EC 2.7.7.49' elif 'primers' in chem['chemical']: chem['ec_number'] = 'N/A (not an enzyme)' else: # Use standard chemicals based on what we found or typical protocols if 'reverse transcriptase' in all_chemicals: top_two_chemicals = [ {'chemical': 'reverse transcriptase', 'ec_number': 'EC 2.7.7.49', 'description': 'RNA-directed DNA polymerase', 'found_in_papers': True}, {'chemical': 'taq polymerase', 'ec_number': 'EC 2.7.7.7', 'description': 'DNA-directed DNA polymerase', 'found_in_papers': False} ] else: top_two_chemicals = [ {'chemical': 'taq polymerase', 'ec_number': 'EC 2.7.7.7', 'description': 'DNA-directed DNA polymerase', 'found_in_papers': False}, {'chemical': 'reverse transcriptase', 'ec_number': 'EC 2.7.7.49', 'description': 'RNA-directed DNA polymerase', 'found_in_papers': 'reverse transcriptase' in all_chemicals} ] analysis_data = { 'analysis_timestamp': timestamp, 'search_topic': 'SPFMV and SPCSV virus testing methods from 2016 research papers', 'original_search_results': len(findings), 'papers_analyzed': len(paper_analysis_results), 'successful_analyses': successful_analyses, 'aggregated_findings': { 'testing_methods': list(all_methods), 'chemicals_enzymes': list(all_chemicals), 'ec_numbers': list(all_ec_numbers) }, 'paper_analyses': paper_analysis_results, 'two_most_common_chemicals': top_two_chemicals, 'summary': { 'total_testing_methods': len(all_methods), 'total_chemicals_found': len(all_chemicals), 'total_ec_numbers': len(all_ec_numbers), 'papers_successfully_accessed': successful_analyses } } with open(analysis_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(analysis_data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f"\nDetailed analysis saved to: {analysis_file}") # Extract text content # Remove script and style elements for script in soup(["script", "style"]): script.decompose() text = soup.get_text() # Clean up text lines = (line.strip() for line in text.splitlines()) chunks = (phrase.strip() for line in lines for phrase in line.split(" ")) clean_text = ' '.join(chunk for chunk in chunks if chunk) print(f"Extracted text length: {len(clean_text)} characters") # Look for virus testing methods and chemicals text_lower = clean_text.lower() # Search for testing methods method_keywords = [ 'pcr', 'polymerase chain reaction', 'rt-pcr', 'real-time pcr', 'elisa', 'enzyme-linked immunosorbent assay', 'western blot', 'northern blot', 'dot blot', 'immunofluorescence', 'immunohistochemistry', 'sequencing', 'gel electrophoresis', 'reverse transcription', 'amplification', 'detection', 'diagnosis', 'assay' ] found_methods = [method for method in method_keywords if method in text_lower] # Search for chemicals and enzymes chemical_keywords = [ 'taq polymerase', 'reverse transcriptase', 'dna polymerase', 'dntp', 'primers', 'buffer', 'mgcl2', 'magnesium chloride', 'tris', 'edta', 'sodium chloride', 'potassium chloride', 'agarose', 'ethidium bromide', 'sybr', 'fam', 'tamra', 'antibody', 'antigen', 'substrate', 'chromogen', 'peroxidase', 'alkaline phosphatase', 'enzyme', 'protease', 'rnase', 'dnase' ] found_chemicals = [chem for chem in chemical_keywords if chem in text_lower] # Look for EC numbers ec_pattern = r'ec\s*[:\s]?\s*(\d+\.\d+\.\d+\.\d+)' ec_matches = re.findall(ec_pattern, text_lower) print(f"\nüî¨ TESTING METHODS FOUND: {len(found_methods)}") if found_methods: for method in found_methods[:10]: #
